subject,\n// and if true, the index of the first subject that applies\nfunc appliesTo(user user.Info, bindingSubjects []rbacv1.Subject, namespace string) (int, bool) {\n\tfor i, bindingSubject := range bindingSubjects {\n\t\tif appliesToUser(user, bindingSubject, namespace) {\n\t\t\treturn i, true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn 0, false\n}\n\nfunc has(set []string, ele string) bool {\n\tfor _, s := The RBACAuthorizer has methods for both authorization (Authorize) and retrieving user rules (RulesFor).\\n\\n## Rule Resolution and Subject Evaluation\\n\\nThe **DefaultRuleResolver** (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go) resolves PolicyRules for a user in a given namespace by:\\n- Implementing RulesFor() which returns all applicable rules\\n- Implementing VisitRulesFor() for iterative rule evaluation\\n- Implementing GetRoleReferenceRules() to resolve role references in bindings\\n- Supporting both cluster-wide and namespace-scoped bindings\\n\\nThe **SubjectAccessEvaluator** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go) identifies which subjects (users, groups, service accounts) can perform an action by examining all role bindings and evaluating their rules against request attributes.\\n\\n## Subject Access Review Handlers\\n\\nMultiple REST handlers process authorization review requests:\\n- **SubjectAccessReview** (pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go) -
